<h1><a name="_Toc361871682"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第一章 <span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>前言</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871682'></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.25pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>讨论组地址</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>: <span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span></span><span lang=EN-US><a
href="http://groups.google.com/group/antlr_chinese/"><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>http://groups.google.com/group/antlr_chinese/</span></a></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.25pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>仔细数起来</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,coding</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>生涯也有不少年头了</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>99</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>年到现在</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>虽然中途离开过几年</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>但始终没有停留过关注</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在这不长不短的岁月里</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在指尖流过的语言也有不少了</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从学生年代的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>c/<span class=SpellE>cpp,object</span>
<span class=SpellE>pascal,asm,sql</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等到工作中用过的</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>vbs</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>/<span class=SpellE>js,java,html,xml</span>,
<span class=SpellE>schema,R,erlang</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和一些即兴学的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>shell script</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等，年轻时偏执于语言的表层，略显轻狂</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>并以之为傲。后来修习图灵机，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lambda</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>算子</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>组合子之类的计算模型，尝试着对语言的本质做了一些深入的思考</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>才发觉其实自己一直都是井底之蛙。在接触了古老的</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lex</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> +<span class=SpellE>yacc</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>后</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>为其高度抽象的简洁与优美所折服</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>遂不能自拔。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一直都比较喜欢类似</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lex+yacc</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>之类产生式工具，由于工作主要是</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>java</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>相关的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>也接触了</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>并对其保持比较浓厚的兴趣</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>时隔几年后重回</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>it</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>时</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>因为一个小产品的开发需要，对词法语法解析工具选型，选了几个工具，</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>javacc</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>jflex+CUP</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，最终还是选择了</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>关于工具的选择方面</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>. </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一直认为</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>工欲善其事，必先利其器，但何为利器，如何评价，一直没有清晰的定义，有些东西，明明很好很强大，但是就是无法推广，比如基于强大</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lambda</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>算子的函数式语言及其平台如</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lisp </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>schema </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等。很多年后，才明白，评价一个一个东西，不仅仅看点上的表现，还需要看面上的表现，比如周边的环境支撑等</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，哪怕点上的表现稍逊一筹，只要面上的表现优异，也能弥补其缺陷。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一个工具，被选择的首当其冲的标准当属于其生产能力，评价选择一个工具的生产能力，除了要看它的主要功能外，还要看它对你的生产流程的覆盖程度。覆盖的越全，也就认为其产出效率越高。凭借</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>eclipse</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这个强大的工具平台。</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>Antlr</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>做到了从前端语法设计到调试到集成测试的无缝覆盖，这确实是我选择其的一个关键决定因素。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>贸然的使用一个不成熟的工具，或者没有实践过的新解决方案，不管它在别人那里是如何成功的，你都需要支付一定风险的。利器从来都是双刃的，伤人亦能伤己，用的好，强虏灰飞烟灭，用的不好，伤痕累累，欲罢不能。诚然，形式化的产生式编程方式如</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>antlr</span></span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的确有其强大且简洁优雅的一面，但凡事有利必有弊，一旦遇到问题，其背后隐藏的抽象的复杂度足够让一个项目或产品栽倒在时间压力面前。这也是这个工具鲜被采用的原因。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>开发结束后</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>对使用这个工具所遇到的问题以及一些解决方法，作了一些总结和整理。前车之鉴，后事之师，不管是为人还是为己。于是萌生了写个文档的想法，说是写，实际上是不过是将所找的零碎资料拼装而已。在找资料的过程中发现，鲜有中文教程，只有一本</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>v2.75</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的中文版规范。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>虽然官方的英文文档不算少，但对于在非英语母语的我们来说，对英文信息的敏感度较低，从那堆信息里，寻找一条合适的学习路径略显艰难。于是就学习吾友陈民的做法，尽力写一些教程像他以前帮助我一样帮助其他人。另外在这里也特别感谢甘草同志</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(healer.kx.yu@gmail.com)</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，加入这个阵营</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>…<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这篇教程定位为帮助零基础的初学者入门到掌握编译前端，为熟悉</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的人，提供一些问题备忘录，以及共享一些对</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>本身设计的看法。希望能对您有所帮助。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc361871683"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第二章 <span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>安装篇</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871683'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:</span></span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>选择</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>确实有很大的优势。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>有官方自带的</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，有</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>民间的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrv3ide </span><span

lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span class=SpellE>netbeans</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>什么的插件等等。还有一些收费的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>eclipse</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>插件等，具体就不去细列了，这个教程主要集中在</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> antlrv3ide+eclipse</span><span

mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等两个</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span class=SpellE>ide</span> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>上面。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>通过本篇的学习，你应该能搭建好一个可以实战的平台。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc361871684"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第一节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>安装前的检查</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871684'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:</span></span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871685"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第1小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>是否已经安装了</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871685'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>java 1.5 </span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871685'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者更高的版本。</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc361871685'></span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p class=MsoListParagraph><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>确认方法</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> java Cversion </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和</span><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>javac</span></span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> Cversion</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，如果不能工作，或者版本不对，请检查环境变量的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>JAVA_HOME<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871686"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第2小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>是否已经下载了</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871686'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>eclipse 3.x.</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>教程使用的是</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> eclipse 3.6.2(<span class=SpellE>helios</span>)<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:"微软雅黑","sans-serif";
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:
微软雅黑;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>Eclipse Modeling Tools</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>那个版本，最好保持和教程一致的。不能确定</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrv3ide</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>是否适用了</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>gef</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>gmf</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>但建议如果你使用其它的类型的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>eclipse </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，将</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>modeling </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>模块升级到最新版本。同时还需要安装一个</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>dynamic languages toolkit core
frameworks.</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这个是</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>antlrv3ide</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>依赖的插件</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>.</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>本教程所用的插件如下</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>（画圈圈的是没有安装插件前就要存在的。如果没有，你需要在</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> help-&gt;install new software </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>中选择</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span class=SpellE>helios</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这个更新源进行更新）</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871687"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第3小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>建立本教程演示目录。</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc361871687'></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>建立一个目录</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>(d:\antlrdemo),</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>用作本教程的演示目录，这个目录可以更换到其他的地方，<span style='color:red'>但是请注意，请不要带有中文或者其他非英文字母</span>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在</span><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>anltrdemo</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>下面建立一个</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks_data</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>目录。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>将</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>eclipse</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>拷贝至</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> <span class=SpellE>antlrdemo</span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>目录下。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>并在</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>eclipse</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>目录下建立</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>
</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>一个</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>workspace</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的目录，并在启动</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>eclipse</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的时候，将工作空间设置为这个目录的工作空间。这样做的目的便于管理资料。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><v:shape id="_x0000_i1065" type="#_x0000_t75"
 style='width:203.25pt;height:228.75pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image002.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:18.0pt;mso-add-space:auto'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>就绪之后，来开始我们的安装过程。。。</span><span lang=EN-US

<h2><a name="_Toc361871688"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

<h3><a name="_Toc361871690"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第2小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>下载</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871690'><span

<h3><a name="_Toc361871692"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第4小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>确认你的安装是否正确。</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc361871692'></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>确认</span><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks</span></span><span lang=EN-US

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>双击</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，如果看到可视界面，就</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>ok</span><span style='font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>了。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>确认</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，安装插件成功后，</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>可以看到</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><v:shape id="图片_x0020_25" o:spid="_x0000_i1058"

</v:shape></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>看到这个，差不多就安装正确了</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>. </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>到目前为止，</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrdemo</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>目录有两个目录：</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>eclipse </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks_data</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和两个</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>jar</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>文件</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>: antlrworks-1.4.2.jar </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr-3.3-complete.jar;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc361871693"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第三章 <span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>工具环境介绍篇：</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871693'></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>虽然一般的开发里面用</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrv3ide</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>就足够了，但是，个人觉得</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在调试语法的时候比较清爽。而且</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrv3ide</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>不能显示抽象语法树，但</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>可以，所以，一般都是双管齐下。前期的语法规则分析和调试之类的，就用</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，涉及到语义动作相关，需要嵌入代码的时候，就切入</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrv3ide </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

  minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
  ZH-CN'>可以和在</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>eclipse</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
  ZH-CN'>上面开发的项目无缝集成在一起。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
  ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>作为初级阶段，这里的使用篇就以经典的表达式解析来展现。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>就绪后，就开始我们的使用之旅吧</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>…<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>通过本篇的学习，你应该可以运行示例的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>demo</span><span

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>文件，并了解工具的各部分的构成。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc361871694"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>先从</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871694'><span

<h3><a name="_Toc361871695"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<h4><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>可选一</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks_data</span></span><span

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

<h4><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

<span class=SpellE>System.err.println</span>(&quot;undefined variable &quot;+$<span

<h3><a name="_Toc361871696"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>之后，还需要输入<span style='color:red'>一个回车换行。</span></span><span

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

<h2><a name="_Toc361871697"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第二节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>再开始品尝</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871697'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>anltrv3ide</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871698"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第1小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>新建一个</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871698'><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871698'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>项目</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871698'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.</span></span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>新建一个名叫</span><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrdemo</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>java</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>项目</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>增加两个目录叫</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>grammar </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lib</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，并将</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr.3.3-complete.jar</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:

<h3><a name="_Toc361871700"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第3小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>进行或者检查插件的设置</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc361871700'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>..</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在</span><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrdemo</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>上右键，选择</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>properties </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，在弹出来的对话框中，左边选择</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span class=SpellE>antlr</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，在右边钩上</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>enable xxx</span><span

<h3><a name="_Toc361871701"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

ZH-CN'>, </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>则会在</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:

mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的源码文件</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
