<h2><a name="_Toc361871702"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第三节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
</span></span></span><![endif]></a><span class=SpellE><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc361871702'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>Antlrworks</span></span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871702'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>工具的各部分使用说明</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc361871702'></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><v:shape id="图片_x0020_52" o:spid="_x0000_i1037"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:415.5pt;height:250.5pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image030.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>语法元素大纲图</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>将语法文件的语法元素以大纲的方式列在左边。上面还有一个左右箭头按钮，用来在语法元素间切换的。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>语法文件编辑器：</span></b><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>编辑语法文件，与普通的编辑器无异，多了一个输入时，会自动对齐的功能。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>语法高亮按钮：</span></b><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>控制语法编辑器是否高亮显示语法关键字。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>调试快速按钮</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这个可以在菜单中找到，但经常用，就列在了界面上。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>调试按钮</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>调试时候，进行单步前进，单步后退，回到最开始位置，或者执行到最后位置。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>中断事件激发点：</span></b><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>设置什么时候进行发出调试中断陷阱信号给调试器。默认设置为</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>token</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>消耗时，也就是当一个词法被识别出来的时候，形成一个</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>token</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>被语法调用消耗时，触发调试中断陷阱。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>输入</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>/</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>输出窗口</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>输入输出窗口共用一块显示区域，不能同时显示，任意一个时间，最多只能显示其中的一个。输入输出窗口的作用主要是关于输入流的显示和被辨认出来的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>token</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>流的输出，由于是</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>ll</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(k)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>算法</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US>( <span class=SpellE>ll</span>(k)
</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的意思是</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>&nbsp;scans input from left-to-right, produces a leftmost derivation top-down,
k symbols of <span class=SpellE>lookahead</span> .</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>而</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lr</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(k)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的意思是</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>a grammar in which purser scans
the input from left to right and generate the reverse rightmost derivation, and
it can take a decision about reduction by looking next k symbol only. That is
why; it is called LR (k) grammar.),</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>所以这两者几乎都是同步的，但由于可能会存在一些</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>token</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>被</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>skip</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>hide</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>了，所以，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>output</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的窗口内容会少于</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>input</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>窗口内容。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>分析树和抽象语法树窗口</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>以树状的形式来展现解析的结果，分析树贴近源语法，是源语法的一个直接映射，抽象语法语法树是对源语法进行抽象后的一个体现。比如，一般整数和实数，在分析树中会对应不同的类型，但是在抽象语法树中，可能会被抽象成操作数这样的统一类型。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>堆栈和事件窗口</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>堆栈窗口展现语法规则被访问的深度关系。就像函数的调用堆栈一样。事件窗口展现每一步发生的事件，比如进入那一个规则，消耗那一些</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>token</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>语法图窗口</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>默认以</span><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>bnf</span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>图方式展示语法规则。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>Show <span class=SpellE>nfa</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>可以选择是否显示非确定型状态机。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><v:shape id="图片_x0020_1" o:spid="_x0000_i1036"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:414.75pt;height:105pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image031.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>解释器窗口</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>可以单独调试某一条规则。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc361871703"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第四节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>Antlrv3ide</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871703'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>插件的各部分使用说明</span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871703'></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>双击</span><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>Expr.g</span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>文件，即可进入</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrv3ide</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的插件关联的视图。下面是各组成部分的说明。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>语法编辑器区：这部分只是辅助编辑</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.g</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的语法文件。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><v:shape id="图片_x0020_4" o:spid="_x0000_i1035"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:415.5pt;height:265.5pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image032.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>解释调试区</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: </span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这部分可以解释调试各种规则。选择需要调试的的规则，在输入区输入待调试的字符串，</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>点击运行按钮，就可以在输出区看到具体语法树或者问题了。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>如果有需要，还可以以新建用例的方式将该次测试保存为</span><span class=SpellE><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>gunit</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>测试用例。以供多次测试用。</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>Gunit</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>用例可以转化成</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>junit</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>用例</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>….<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><v:shape id="图片_x0020_7" o:spid="_x0000_i1034"
 type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:415.5pt;height:219pt;visibility:visible;
 mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image033.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA;mso-no-proof:yes'><v:shape id="图片_x0020_10" o:spid="_x0000_i1033"

</v:shape></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc361871704"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第四章 <span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>使用篇</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871704'></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在安装完成后，并通过简单的使用，熟悉了</span><span class=SpellE><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>工具</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrworks</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>以及插件</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlrv3ide</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的各部分，已利其器了，剩下的就是如何欲善其事了。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>本篇的安排拟这样</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>先吹吹水，了解一下一些历史典故，然后对一些基本概念作一个大体介绍，对经典的表达式进行剖析，再安排一个具体的场景《状态机代码生成框架》，中间会穿插一些编译原理知识。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>通过本篇的学习后，你应该能够使用</span><span class=SpellE><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>把工作中需求转化成设计，如果不能，就给我来</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>email</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>吧，我们一起探讨一下如何改进这个教程。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc361871705"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第一节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>无责任乱弹</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871705'></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一般古代出征时总会祭拜先祖或者什么大神之类的，求乞庇护。这里我们也烧几柱香来拜祭一下相关的先祖们。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>上一个世纪是一个伟人井喷的世纪</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>希尔伯特提出了著名的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>23</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>个著名的问题</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在第二个问题中，并企图建立一套完备的独立的相容的公理体系</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>使得一起的数学命题在这套公理体系内经过有限步骤地推导都能得到真伪的判断，这个世界大同式得梦想让当时所有的数学家都振奋不已。但在</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>1931</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>年，哥德尔不完备定理的出现，让这一共产主义式的梦想破灭。哥德尔令人信服的证明了：任何相容</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>无矛盾</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的公理系统，只要包含初等算术的陈述，必定存在一个不可判定的问题，用这组公理不能判断其真假。也就是说，“相容”和“完备”犹如鱼和熊掌，不可得而兼之。吹开迷雾后才发现理想的公理系统就像一件捉襟见肘的华丽外衣。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>1936</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>年，图灵和邱奇为了第</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>10</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>个问题，分别构造了两种殊途同归的计算模型，图灵机和</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lambda</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>算子</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>貌似还有一个数学家提出了递归函数</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。图灵机以感性直观的方式展现了逻辑的机械性质，而</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lambda</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>算子则以理性的方式揭示了逻辑的抽象变换本质。图灵停机问题和</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lambda</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>算子中的不动点算子</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(Y <span class=SpellE>combinator</span>)</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>为哥德尔德不完备定理提供了有力的佐证。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>图灵机和</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lambda</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>算子之于计算理论与波粒二象性之于物理比较像</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在基本粒子身上同时体现出了两种特性</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>图灵的计算模型将思维的运动转化成了机械的运动方式，为计算机的制造提供了可能。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>1944 </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，冯诺依曼要计算原子弹的反应传播雇佣了</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>100</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>多名女计算员，日以继夜的计算仍然不能满足计算需求，偶然机会他了解到了</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>ENIAC</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>计算机的研制计划，很感兴趣，改造了一下，用逻辑等价的稳定可靠的基于二进制设计的电路</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>代替了复杂的多进制逻辑电路，成了，然后再给那台机器加了个内存条，就变成了传说中的冯诺依曼机（笑侃，莫当真，冯诺依曼机是指一种结构）。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>有了计算机，自然就催生了程序设计语言，甚至在还没有计算机之前，就已经有了程序员，第一个程序员是一个非常有才华的美女</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<span class=SpellE>Ada</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，拜伦的女儿。这世界上，聪明的女人本来就很少，美丽的聪明女人更是少之又少。可惜英年早逝，三十六岁就</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>down</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>掉了，每每想起此事，未免黯然叹息，天妒红颜阿。但她天才的预见留存来下来，并在之后的一百多年后一一得到验证。每次读到这个</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>ada</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这个单词就</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>仿佛看到在皎洁的月光下，有一名婉约的女子，站在世界之巅瞻望，她火热眼睛里面映照着单调的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>01</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>世界精彩的未来，在那里不仅有子程序，流程图，还有音乐，图画</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>….<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在描述程序设计语言的本身的时候，不可避免地涉及到巴克斯</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>-</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>诺尔范式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>半路出家貌似是很多大拿的路子。或许是因为他们的聪明才智是特地为计算机而生的，之前，都是在为遇见的那一刻准备。巴克斯和诺尔就是这样的仁兄。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>据说巴克斯年少时不爱读书，混了个中学毕业。在大学时由于无知选择了化学，但也没怎么学好</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>...(</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>感谢当年同学的不杀之恩哪。要不编程语言历史得倒退多少年阿</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，不过却年少方刚比较热血，二战时头脑一热跑去当陆军医疗兵了，在这中间检查出了脑瘤，接受了手术。兵是当不成了，鬼子也是打不了了，但光活着也不是办法，于是他想转职做个无线电工了此残生算了。在上岗前的培训中，忽然着了魔般的对数学感兴趣了，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>鬼知道是不是那个脑瘤影响了他大脑的结构</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，后来回炉考研重造，学成后跑去</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>IBM</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，后来的事，大家都知道了</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>....</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>就这样一代天才终于找到了自己的天赋和使命，找到了上帝交给他的任务，开发了第一个高级编程语言，并抽象出了一个描述高级程序设计语言的规范</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>巴克斯范式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>诺尔更是一个意外的客串</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>丫当时根本就没想过要在计算机界闯出个名堂来，而醉心于夜观天象。他本职也是一个天文学家，由于需要处理大量的天文数据，也就被逼成了计算机专家。在巴黎的著名的</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>algol</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>大会上，诺尔大幅度的简化了巴斯克范式，并作为大会总结人用它优雅简洁的描述了</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>algol</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的特性，于是就产生了那份在编程语言史上有划时代意义的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>算法语言</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>algol60</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>报告</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，这个报告展示了从接近人类语言的视角去和机器沟通，而不是用机器语言的视角去和机器沟通的方式。换句话说，他们成功的让所有的开发活动从以机器为中心转移到了以人的逻辑思维为中心，从此解放了机器特性对人的思维逻辑的束缚，这是个了不起的质的飞跃，就像从活着是为了吃饭跃迁到吃饭是为了活着的境界。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>诺尔还是一个才华横溢的人，足迹涉及了天文学，心理学，生物学，古典音乐等，但在其他领域都不如他在计算机上的名声大，后来也就慢慢的专业搞计算机了。还有一点有意思的是，诺尔虽然得了图灵奖，但却始终不承认图灵关于人工智能的想法。世界上的事往往都是这么赶巧，无心插柳的，却荫了一大片。宿命阿。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt;tab-stops:125.0pt'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>接着该到乔姆斯基出场了。我眼中的乔大叔堪比金庸笔下的风清扬。他虽然不是计算机科学家，只是哲学家和语言学家，但他成功地把语法结构统一到了状态机的计算模型上来，向世人揭示了语法的数学本质。在没有看到乔姆斯基的形式文法前，我从未意识到感性的语言还有这么理性的内涵。当然这中间可能很多都是来自于他的老师哈里斯关于语言结构</span><span
lang=EN-US><a
href="http://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E7%BA%BF%E6%80%A7%E7%AE%97%E5%AD%90"
title=线性算子><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
color:windowtext;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;text-decoration:none;text-underline:
none'><span lang=EN-US>线性算子</span></span></a></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>方面的发现。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>好了，祭祀大典结束</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>...</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>接下来我们该分猪肉了。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc361871706"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第二节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>关于语法解析的一些基本概念</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc361871706'></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>虽然现代语文到处都是主谓宾什么的，但是很奇怪，在古代却鲜有分析语法的，说文解字的很多，谋篇布局的也很多，可是研究语法的却很少，貌似这是一个很自然的事情，这件事确实好玩，古人的文章都是没有标点的，全靠语义断句，和现代的先判断语法再判断语义几乎是违背的。后来马建忠照着西方的语法研究体系框架，对中文做了一个全面的审视，横空出了一本</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>马氏文通</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，奠定了现代汉语研究的基础。但是这种词本位的研究方法，终究不是太合适，以至于到了现在，都还没有一种靠谱的分词方法，那些号称准确到</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>95%</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>以上的多数都是基于统计的方法，也就是说，它们的本质基本都是基于现有使用频率而定，不具备推导性。我隐隐约约的感觉到</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(<span class=SpellE>ps</span>:</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>只是隐隐约约的感觉到</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，中文体系的机制有点类似</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>lambda</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>算子，英文体系的机制有点象图灵机体系。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>:) </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>扯了那么多，是想告诉你</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>... </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>本教程不打算研究中文，哈哈。如果你打算做中文语法解析，下面的内容，你可以不用看了。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>本篇并不打算以严格的形式介绍编译原理的前端的内容，因为，严格的话也是抄龙虎鲸书等</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>而且，愿意啃哪几本书的，基本也用不着本教程了。也就从需求的角度信手即乱弹了。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>通常，我们要表达一个系统的观点，都会用文章来表达，一篇文章，是由若干个段落组成，</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>段落是有若干有逻辑联系的句子组成。句子是有若干词语构成的，就像一层一层的洋葱。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>词语或者叫单词就是那些无法再拆分的最小的具有概念意义的单位。词语是由字母有序组成的，但字母不具备概念意义。到了这里，就有了一条严格的分水线了</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.... </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>以单词为分界线，单词之上的，组成结构的元素都是具有概念意义的。单词以下，组成结构的元素都是没有概念意义的。（请再一次注意，我说的是英文体系的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>...</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>不是中文体系</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>) </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>于是这里就引出了两个概念，词法分析和语法分析。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871707"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第1小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>什么是词法分析，什么是语法分析，这两者有什么不同？</span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871707'></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>词法分析</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一门研究无意义的字母如何组成有意义的单词的技术。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>语法分析</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一门研究有意义的单词如何组成更复杂意义的句子，文章的技术。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>例子</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span class=SpellE>hello,my</span>
name is <span class=SpellE>alan</span>, <span class=SpellE>i</span> come from
china.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>以上是一个自我介绍的片段。</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>词法分析是识别出一个一个的单词</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>比如</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>hello</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> my</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等。</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>单个的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> h</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>e ,<span class=SpellE>l,l,o</span>
</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>是不具备概念意义的，</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>只有有序组成</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>hello</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的时候才具备一个概念意义。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>那语法分析又是什么呢？</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>我们假定这是一个标准的自我介绍的文章。这个文章由三段组成：问候语，名字介绍，归属地介绍</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> :) . <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>问候语采用</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> hello </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> hello xxx </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的形式。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>名字介绍采用</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>my name is xxx </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的形式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>归属地介绍采用</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> <span class=SpellE>i</span> come from xxx</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的形式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>那我们规定的这种标准介绍的格式，就是所谓的语法，每一条叫语法规则。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>我们通常意义上的英文语法，本质上也是这样的，但他们的语法结构层次多点，各组成部分的划分多些和标准些。我们常说的英语句式，就是所谓的语法，但是语法不仅仅包括句式，还包括篇章段落结构等。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>比如一个最简单的英语句式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>主语谓语宾语。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>主语由名词或者代词组成。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>谓语由动词组成。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>宾语由名词或者代词组成。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>以下为简单起见就假设各个结构组成成分最多只有两个吧。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>名词：</span></b><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>专有名词或者普通名词。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>参见</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>http://baike.baidu.com/view/26580.htm)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>专有名词：常见的人名或者地名</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>也见字典的专有名词列表。如</span><b><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>China</span></b><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>（</span><span
lang=EN-US><a href="http://baike.baidu.com/view/61891.htm" target="_blank"><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span lang=EN-US>中国</span></span></a></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>）、</span><b><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>Asia</span></b><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>（</span><span
lang=EN-US><a href="http://baike.baidu.com/view/2918.htm" target="_blank"><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span lang=EN-US>亚洲</span></span></a></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>）</span><b><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>Beijing</span></b><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>（</span><span

mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span lang=EN-US>北京</span></span></a></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
