mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>）</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>普通名词</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>个体名词或者物质名词。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>个体名词</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: </span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>单个人或者物的名词，如</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>car </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>汽车</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> room </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>房间</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> fan </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>风扇</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>photo </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>照片等。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>物质名词</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: </span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>表示物质或不具备确定形状和大小的个体的物质。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>fire </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>火</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> steel </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>钢</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> air </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空气</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> water </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>水</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> milk</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>牛奶。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>动词</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:</span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>表示动作的词语。</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一般见字典的动词表，比如</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>is </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>do</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> make </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等等。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>代词</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: it</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>i</span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> she</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>he</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等词语。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>也就是说，这个经过阉割的简单的主谓宾的句式，语法结构是这样的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><v:shape id="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75"
 style='width:371.25pt;height:155.25pt' o:ole="">
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image035.emz" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OLEObject Type="Embed" ProgID="Visio.Drawing.11" ShapeID="_x0000_i1025"
  DrawAspect="Content" ObjectID="_1435613669">
 </o:OLEObject>
</xml><![endif]--></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>椭圆框内的是字母序列，是具体的单词例子。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>方框是作为语法分析的基本单位，是词法分析出来的最后终结果。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>圆角框是符合的语法结构。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>像</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> it is tree </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，就是这样的结构。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><v:shape id="_x0000_i1026" type="#_x0000_t75"
 style='width:176.25pt;height:155.25pt' o:ole="">
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image036.emz" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>

  DrawAspect="Content" ObjectID="_1435613670">
 </o:OLEObject>
</xml><![endif]--></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>那如何来描述词法语法规则呢？</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这就涉及到了鼎鼎有名的巴克斯</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>-</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>诺尔范式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871708"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第2小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>巴克斯</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>-</span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>诺尔范式</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>产生式</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>最左推导</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>最右推导</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>左递归</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>右递归</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871708'></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>巴克斯发明了一种叫巴克斯范式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(<span
class=langwithname>Backus Normal Form</span>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的格式来标示语法词法，语法词法本质上其实是一样的，不过是组成单位是否有逻辑概念意义而已。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>巴克斯范式后经诺尔改进，后人便合成巴克斯</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>-</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>诺尔范式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'> </span>(</span><span class=langwithname><span
lang=EN-US>Backus-Naur Form</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>简称都是叫</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>BNF</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>这个范式很简单</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>见</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>http://zh.wikipedia.org/zh-cn/%E5%B7%B4%E7%A7%91%E6%96%AF%E8%8C%83%E5%BC%8F)</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>规定了一个语法结构的描述是由一堆语法规则组成，</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>每一个规则符合这样的格式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>符号</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&gt; ::= &lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>使用符号的表达式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&gt;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>这里的</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> &lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>符号</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&gt; </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>是非终结符，而表达式由一个符号序列，或用指示选择的竖杠</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> '|' </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>分隔的多个符号序列构成，<span
style='color:red'>每个符号序列整体都是左端的符号的一种可能的替代</span>。<span style='color:red'>从未在左端出现的符号叫做终结符</span>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>具体可以解读成</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>非终结符</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&gt; ::= &lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>可能选择表达式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>1&gt; | &lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>可能选择表达式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>2&gt;...<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>BNF</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在描述上是存在着一些缺陷的，</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>它无力描述它所占用的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&lt;&gt; ::= | </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等字符，用现在的话说是没有转义功能。另外，它对可选结构</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>可有可无的选项</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>以及重复项的描述很罗嗦。于是就有了</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>EBNF(</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>扩展巴克斯范式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的出现。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>具体看</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(http://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E6%89%A9%E5%B1%95%E5%B7%B4%E7%A7%91%E6%96%AF%E8%8C%83%E5%BC%8F).<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>现在常用的，基本都</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>EBNF</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的格式，但</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>BNF</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>EBNF </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>两者能力等价。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一般采用产生式来做语法推导，可以认为产生式其实就是</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>BNF</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的一条规则的另一种表达方式。产生式采用</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>前提条件</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>-&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>结论动作</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这样的表达方式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>采用这种产生式的规则，可以很好的诠释语法的推导过程。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>比如有一个这样的规则集合</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>{S-&gt;AB,A-&gt;a, B-&gt;b } </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>要分析的字符串</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> SB<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>最左推导是</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>SB-&gt;ABB-&gt;<span class=SpellE>aBB</span>-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>abB</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>abb</span>;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>最右推导是</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>SB-&gt;<span class=SpellE>Sb</span>-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>ABb</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>Abb</span>-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>abb</span>;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>他们的区别是很简单的</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从左边还是从右边开始按照规则替换。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在替换的过程中，可能会遭遇左递归或者右递归的情况，左递归是相对最左推导而产生的，右递归是相对最右推导而产生的。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>举例说明</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,{A-&gt;<span class=SpellE>Aa,A</span>-&gt;b}<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>当使用最左推导时，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>A-&gt;<span class=SpellE>Aa</span>,</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>就会陷入无限的分裂中</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> A-&gt;AAA...a</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。经典的处理方法是将这两个产生式转换成</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>3</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>个等价的产生式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{A-&gt;<span class=SpellE>bR,R</span>-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>aR,R</span>-&gt;</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>}; </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>具体可以自行验证一下，编译原理的书也有详细叙述。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:auto'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>右递归也类似这样。不过是形如</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(A-&gt;<span class=SpellE>aA,A</span>-&gt;b)</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的产生式规则</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在运用最右推导的时候才会产生，解决方法也雷同。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871709"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第3小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;font-weight:normal;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>语法解析的</span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871709'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>自顶向下和自底向上的策略</span></span><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc361871709'></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>语法解析的过程，就算是拿这个纸带似的字符串序列按照一定规则扭成目标的语法结构，如果能扭成，就说明这个是字符串序列是符合这个语法的，否则就是不符合这个语法的。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>那现在我们关注一下这个扭的过程。一般而言，有以下两种策略。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>自顶向下的策略：在构造语法树</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>就是那个像一颗倒着的树的语法结构</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的时候，从语法树的根节点开始，按照先根顺序构造各个节点，也就是说，叶结点总是后于根节点创建，</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>过程就像从上面</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>根节点</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>到下面</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>叶结点</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>建造，因此得名。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>自底向上，刚好相反。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>如何理解这两者的区别呢？</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一个人，左手拿着一个语法结构，右手从一个管道里面取出</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>输入字符串的积木块。往语法结构里面叠放，最后叠出来了带输入字符串的语法结构，这个就叫自顶向下。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>如果那个人左手拿着一段输入字符串，右手从一堆</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>零散的语法结构积木块里面取出合适的积木块，往输入字符串上叠放，最后得到一个带输入字符串的语法结构，这个就叫自底向上。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>我们玩一个</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>A</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>说</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>B</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>说得游戏来具体说明这个过程吧。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>我们定义这样的语法结构</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>句式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>DEMO: </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>主语</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>谓语</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>宾语</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>主语</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>人名，简单的以</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>&quot;A&quot; &quot;B&quot; ...&quot;Z&quot;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>来命名。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>谓语</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: &quot;say&quot; </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span
lang=EN-US>&quot;is&quot; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>两个动词。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>宾语</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: that</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从句</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US>&quot;over&quot;</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这个词。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从句：</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&quot;that&quot; </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>主语</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>谓语</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>宾语。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>现在我们来分析</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这样的一个句子</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>A say
that B say that C is over;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>先来看看自顶向上是怎样的过程：</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>我们先略去词法分析，假设</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>A B C say is that over</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这些已经被识别为单词</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>左手拿着语法结构</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>句式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>demo<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，右手准备从管道里面取出单词。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>句式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>demo </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>要求的第一个元素是</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>主语：人名。</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>右手从管道里面取出的第一个单词是</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>A </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，刚好是人名，两者符合，于是到下一步，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><v:shape id="_x0000_i1027" type="#_x0000_t75"
 style='width:102pt;height:87pt' o:ole="">
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image037.emz" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OLEObject Type="Embed" ProgID="Visio.Drawing.11" ShapeID="_x0000_i1027"
  DrawAspect="Content" ObjectID="_1435613671">
 </o:OLEObject>
</xml><![endif]--></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>句式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>demo </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>要求第二个元素是</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>谓语</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> say </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> is </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>两个单词。</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>
</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>右手从管道取出的第二个单词是</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>
say</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>，</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>也符合要求，于是可以继续下一步。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><v:shape id="_x0000_i1028" type="#_x0000_t75"
 style='width:102pt;height:88.5pt' o:ole="">
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image038.emz" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OLEObject Type="Embed" ProgID="Visio.Drawing.11" ShapeID="_x0000_i1028"
  DrawAspect="Content" ObjectID="_1435613673">
 </o:OLEObject>
</xml><![endif]--></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>句式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>demo </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>要求的第三个元素是</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> over </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>以</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>开头的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从句。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>右手从管道取出的是</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that.. </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>满足是</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的从句的特征，但是此刻不能判断是不是正确的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从句，假定为</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从句，跳到</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从句的语法规则，继续下一步。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><v:shape id="_x0000_i1029" type="#_x0000_t75"
 style='width:145.5pt;height:119.25pt' o:ole="">
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image039.emz" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OLEObject Type="Embed" ProgID="Visio.Drawing.11" ShapeID="_x0000_i1029"
  DrawAspect="Content" ObjectID="_1435613674">
 </o:OLEObject>
</xml><![endif]--></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从句要求</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>that</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>之后的元素是</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>主语</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>人名。右手从管道里面取出的是</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>B </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，符合要求，继续下一步</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>...<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>重复以上步骤，刚刚好左手所有用到的规则都得到满足，而右手管道的内容也都空了。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>于是我们就得到了这样的一棵语法结构树</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><v:shape id="_x0000_i1030" type="#_x0000_t75"
 style='width:325.5pt;height:219.75pt' o:ole="">
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image040.emz" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OLEObject Type="Embed" ProgID="Visio.Drawing.11" ShapeID="_x0000_i1030"
  DrawAspect="Content" ObjectID="_1435613675">
 </o:OLEObject>
</xml><![endif]--></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>我们再来看看自底向上的过程</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>把上面过程的左右手换过来</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>左手字符串的管道，右手语法规则堆。我们借助一种叫堆栈的结构工具，你可以把堆栈想象成像</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>子弹夹这样的东西，后压进去的子弹先出来，如果有子弹的话，永远有一颗子弹保持在顶端，我们把那个顶端位置叫做栈顶。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>自底向上的处理过程总体是这样的，把左手的字符串中的元素按照顺序，像子弹一样，一个一个的压入进去，压入一个就从栈顶开始依次往栈底检查，如果符合右边语法规则堆里面的规则，就把符合部分的堆栈内容弹出，把那个抽象规则名，压入进去，</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>把字符串压入栈的过程叫<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>移动</b>，发现符合语法规则，变成抽象的语法名称实例</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>handle) ,</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>然后再压入栈的过程叫<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>规约</b>。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>具体例子过程如下</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><v:shape id="_x0000_i1031" type="#_x0000_t75"
 style='width:414.75pt;height:667.5pt' o:ole="">
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image041.emz" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OLEObject Type="Embed" ProgID="Visio.Drawing.11" ShapeID="_x0000_i1031"
  DrawAspect="Content" ObjectID="_1435613676">
 </o:OLEObject>
</xml><![endif]--></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><v:shape id="_x0000_i1032" type="#_x0000_t75"
 style='width:415.5pt;height:345pt' o:ole="">
 <v:imagedata src="hand%20in%20hand%20with%20antlr.files/image042.emz" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><!--[if gte mso 9]><xml>
 <o:OLEObject Type="Embed" ProgID="Visio.Drawing.11" ShapeID="_x0000_i1032"
  DrawAspect="Content" ObjectID="_1435613677">
 </o:OLEObject>
</xml><![endif]--></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc361871710"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第三节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>经典的表达式教程解析</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc361871710'></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>几乎每一本语法解析的教程都会用整数四则表达式来当作入门级别的语法教程，这节就以实用的视角去剖析这个教程，我们就当它是一个真实的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>case</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>吧。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871711"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第1小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>界定需求</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871711'></span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>假设你给某一个程序一串常用的三则混合运算的表达式，要求这个程序给你计算出结果，显示的要求如下</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:26.5pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo13'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>1)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>使用者传递文本传递文本给程序，程序解析完后在控制台输出结果，或者错误信息</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:26.5pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo13'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>2)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>输入和结果为整型范围的整数。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:26.5pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo13'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>3)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>支持命名的表达式。表达式结果可以被其他表达式按名引用。支持多条表达式批量计算。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:26.5pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo13'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
