mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>4)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>支持加减乘三种运算符号</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>符号操作意义同数学，注</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>乘优先级比加减高。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:26.5pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l3 level1 lfo13'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>5)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>支持括号，括号改变原有的运算符号优先级。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:26.5pt;mso-add-space:auto'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这个</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>case</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>比较特殊，它的需求是简单直白的，故没经过什么抽象过程。然而，在真实的环境中，以用户用例界定功能边界，从用例中抽取出需求。这是一个很重要也很复杂的工作，这也超出了本书的范围与作者的能力，有兴趣的可以看看关于</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>需求的探索</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&gt; &lt;<span class=SpellE>rup</span>&gt;&lt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>分析与设计</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>等软件需求分析与设计的书。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>一般用</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>use case</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>来捕捉描述需求，这里我拟总结出自己的一些经验法则，<span
style='color:red'>但有必要提醒一下，这只是个人经验法则，没有经过严格的证明是对的</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>.</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>请批判性的接受</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>要找出参与者，语言是多方沟通的契约。所以要找出场景中的参与者。并对参与者进行归类。即要抽象出参与者的角色。（见需求</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>1</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>）</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>找出潜在的条件约束，以及沟通的目的，这个对语义实现很重要。比如在实时交易的场景下，对时间的要求很严格，这种就是潜在的约束条件。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>沟通的目的又是什么呢？</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>像表达式的例子的目的就是计算这个表达式最后的结果。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>见需求</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>2)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>抽取出专业术语，这个对词法分析和语义实现很重要。这其实是一种取巧的做法，利用人的思维锤炼出来的结果。当一件事情被锤炼千百遍的时候，人脑一般都会进行抽象，用最精简的信息来描述这个事件，这就是常说的行话。精简的信息包含的大量的内涵，内涵决定了语义的实现。比如行话“调试</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(debug) </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>”就是包含了设置断点一步一步追踪检查程序代码每一处状态的一系列过程。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>见需求</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>3</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>、</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>4)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>明确专业术语要求的上下文。比如隐含某些参数或者需要指定具体的参数，那些术语需要和那些术语配套使用。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>见需求</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>3</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>、</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>4</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>、</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>5)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo21'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>判断描述的粒度。有一些场景，用一个句子就可以描述清楚了，有些场景需要用一段话来描述，而有一些场景，需要用一篇文章来描述。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:auto'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871712"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第2小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>设计语法</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871712'></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>设计语法是一个很麻烦的过程，但也是一个最重要的过程。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;
text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l9 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span></b><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>首先要列出所有的单词项，并设计出词法规则。表达式例子中单词项如下</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: <o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>标识符</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>表达式名，由</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>A</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>到</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>Z</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>组成，位数不限。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>由</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>0</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>到</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>9</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>组成，位数不限，</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>实际上不考虑而已，本例不支持大数</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>).<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>加号</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:+<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>减号</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:-<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>乘号</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:*<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>除号</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:/<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>左括号</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:(<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>右括号</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>:)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>词法规则，实际就是正则表达式来描述，不熟悉的人到网络上搜以下正则表达式的经典教材看看吧。这里不累述了。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l9 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span></b><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>分析使用场景，根据需求，逐步分析出语法推导的产生式规则集合。</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>从一堆杂乱的需求中去构造出精巧准确的语法结构，是一个由简入繁的不断反复迭代的过程，如抽茧剥丝后裁衣一样，大凡此类工作都有一定的艺术鉴赏性，但只有你沉浸其中时才能体味。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>我们观察需求，对语法元素进行分类，按照其作用将涉及元素分成三类</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项，标识符</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>}</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>作为操作项，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>加减乘</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>}</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>作为运算符，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>括号</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>}</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>作为辅助符号。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>我们从每一个分类中取一个元素出来分析，构造出产生式描述的语法规则组。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>然后再逐步的加入同类的元素。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>先取</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项，加法，和括号</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>三个元素。它们只有两种形式，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>+</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>+</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>+....<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:

style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>+(</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>+</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项</span><span

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项</span><span

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:

mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:red;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>假设</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:red;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>a</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:

mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>用这个两条产生式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{S-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>S+a,S</span>-&gt;a} </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>就可以描述第一条语法规则，有人可能会问这两条产生式是如何的，其实我也不知道，貌似自然而然的就抽象出来了，再仔细想了一想，我觉得用数学归纳法比较适合解释这个过程。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>a,a+a,a+a+a,a+a+a+a,a+a+a+a+a</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>....<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>=&gt; a,{a}+a,{<span
class=SpellE>a+a</span>}+a,{<span class=SpellE>a+a+a</span>}+a,{<span
class=SpellE>a+a+a+a</span>}+a....(</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>我们借助花括号来帮助界定成分</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>括号里面的就是前面的式子。然后就推出了通项：</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>A[0]=a<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>A[n] = A[n-1]+a</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>；</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:red;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>请注意：这里的</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:red;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>+</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>是一个字符串符号</span><span lang=EN-US
style='color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>, <span class=SpellE>a+a</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>代表</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>a</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>连接</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>+</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>号连接</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>a</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{S-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>S+a,S</span>-&gt;a} </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>虽然直观却不适合最左推导，按照公式转一下</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>(</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:red;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>见上面的最左推导</span><span

宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:

mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{S-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>aR,R</span>-&gt;+<span class=SpellE>aR,R</span>-&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:

mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>再看第二种形式；</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>通过观测可以看出来，括号里面的是一个子表达式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:

mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>于是</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{S-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>S+a,S</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>a,S</span>-&gt;(S) } <span

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:

mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>转成符合最左推导的形式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:
{ S-&gt;<span class=SpellE>aR,R</span>-&gt;+<span class=SpellE>aR,R</span>-&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,S-&gt;(S)}<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>重新选取</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>整数项，减号，括号，进行同样的分析和构造，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:

mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>可以得到</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>
{S-&gt;S-<span class=SpellE>a,S</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>a,S</span>-&gt;(S)
}<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>由于加减法对等，合并后可以得到</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{S-&gt;S-<span
class=SpellE>a,S</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>S+a,S</span>-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>a,S</span>-&gt;(S) }<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>这就是描述加减混合运算的式子，很容易通过实例来验证的。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>同理的，我们可以把乘法也加入进来</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>,</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>可以得到这样的一个</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{S-&gt;S-<span
class=SpellE>a,S</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>S+a,S</span>-&gt;S*<span
class=SpellE>a,S</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>a,S</span>-&gt;(S) } <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>转成符合最左推导的形式</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:
{ S-&gt;<span class=SpellE>aR,R</span>-&gt;+<span class=SpellE>aR</span>, R-&gt;-<span
class=SpellE>aR</span>, R-&gt;*<span class=SpellE>aR</span> ,R-&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,S-&gt;(S)}<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>如果，我只是说，如果</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>...</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>这个世界上只语法实现语法而不实现语义的话</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>... </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>那就太完美了。但通常上帝都会给你留点遗憾的。这些规则完全可以合法的解析含加减乘的表达式，但是它们无法区分出需求中比较重要的一条</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>乘法优先级比加减的优先级要高。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>乔</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>boss</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>说过一句经典名言：形式应该追随功能。很显然的，我们之前抽象归纳出来的语法规则的形式并不是追随功能的，那就变换一下吧。我们知道乘法的优先级比加减法高，故涉及乘法的表达式部分应该先结合成项，然后再作为加减算术符号的两边的操作项再形成加减表达式，故我们在乘法的基础</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{M-&gt;M*a, M-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>a,M</span>-&gt;(M)}</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>上，垒上一层加减法看看，如下</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{M-&gt;M*a,
M-&gt;<span class=SpellE>a,M</span>-&gt;(M), S-&gt;M+M,S-&gt;M-M}<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>嗯，挺接近了，但这组语法规则无法解决两个问题</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>1</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>、无法处理多个连续的加减号。</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>形如</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>a+a</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>-a-<span class=SpellE>a+a</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>2</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>、从开始符号无法推导纯的连续乘表达式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>3</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>、无法处理子表达式中超过一个加减号的。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>针对问题</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，分析一下特点，第一项必须为</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>a </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，第二项为第一项连接</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>+a </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者第一项连接</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>-a,</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>因此推出通向项为前一项连接上</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>+a</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>或者连接上</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>-a</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，于是我们就大致可以推断出规则</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>引入一个</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>Expr</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>简写为</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>E {E-&gt;M,E-&gt;E+M,E-&gt;E-M}</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>来代替加减项，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>于是得到规则组</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>: {M-&gt;M*a, M-&gt;<span class=SpellE>a,M</span>-&gt;(M), E-&gt;M,E-&gt;E+M,
E-&gt;E-M,S-&gt;E }<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>同时因为加入一个</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>E-&gt;M</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，也解决了问题</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>2</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，即从开始符号推导出连续乘。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>针对问题</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>3</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，把</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>M-&gt;(M) </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>改成</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> M-&gt;(E)</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。也即乘法中要有比乘法范围更广的包含了加减法的子表达式做为因子项，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>于是得到语法规则组</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>{M-&gt;M*a, M-&gt;<span class=SpellE>a,M</span>-&gt;(E), E-&gt;M, E-&gt;E+M,
E-&gt;E-M,S-&gt;E }<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>转化成符合最左推导的语法规则组是</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{ M-&gt;
<span class=SpellE>aR,R</span>-&gt;*<span class=SpellE>aR,R</span>-&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,M-&gt;(E), E-&gt;MN, N-&gt;+MN, N-&gt;-MN,N-&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>,S-&gt;E }<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>至此，整数项，加减乘符，括号已经被加入进来了。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>现在加入标识符号。</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>引入标识符</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>id </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>简写为</span><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>i</span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，</span><span
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>加入标识符后，</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> a </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>和</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> <span class=SpellE>i</span> </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>就成了同等意义的符号，可以抽象出一层，我们使用大写</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>A</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>来代表。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{A-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>a,A</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>i</span>}<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>同时，匿名表达式仍然保持之前同样的语法结构，新增了一个命名表达式，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>所以，用一个新的元素</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>P{P-&gt;E,P-&gt;<span class=SpellE>i</span>=E}</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>来代替，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>于是规则变成</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{ A-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>a,A</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>i,M</span>-&gt;M*a, M-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>a,M</span>-&gt;(E), E-&gt;M, E-&gt;E+M, E-&gt;E-M, P-&gt;E,P-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>i</span>=E, S-&gt;P }<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>转化成符合最左推导的语法规则组是</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{ A-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>a,A</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>i,M</span>-&gt;AR,R-&gt;*AR,R-&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>, M-&gt;(E), E-&gt;MN, N-&gt;+MN,
N-&gt;-MN,N-&gt;</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>, P-&gt;E,P-&gt;<span class=SpellE>i</span>=E,S-&gt;P}<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>至此所有的重要符号都已经加入完成。</span><span style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'> <span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>但对照需求</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>3</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>，还有批量表达式的支持，只需要对</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>P</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的重复即可也即</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{S-&gt;P,S-&gt;SP} </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>最后合并在一起便是</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{ A-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>a,A</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>i,M</span>-&gt;M*a, M-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>a,M</span>-&gt;(E), E-&gt;M, E-&gt;E+M, E-&gt;E-M, P-&gt;E,P-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>i</span>=E, S-&gt;P,S-&gt;SP }<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>转化成符合最优推导的语法规则组</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{ A-&gt;<span
class=SpellE>a,A</span>-&gt;<span class=SpellE>i,M</span>-&gt;AR,R-&gt;*AR,R-&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>, M-&gt;(E), E-&gt;MN, N-&gt;+MN,
N-&gt;-MN,N-&gt;</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>空</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'>, P-&gt;E,P-&gt;<span class=SpellE>i</span>=E,S-&gt;PQ,Q-&gt;PQ,Q-&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:

lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>}<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;tab-stops:193.5pt'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>至此，我们就从需求开始进行一步步地推导得到了最后的语法规则组。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l9 level1 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:
Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span></b><![endif]><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>把语法规则产生式集合转化成</span></b><span
class=SpellE><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
