auto'><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>prog</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>stat+ ;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:
auto'><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-add-space:auto'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>至此最重要的语法设计完成了，对照需求，一步一步地进行推导出产生式规则，最后翻译成</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>antlr</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>所支持的</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>ebnf</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>范式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3><a name="_Toc361871713"><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>第3小节<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>实现语义</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc361871713'></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>在很多的场景里面，具体语法一般要转成抽象语法树，然后再在抽象语法树上实现语义动作，这样做的好处可以避免冗余的处理，不同的语法元素但具有相同的语义含义的，可以转化成统一格式合并处理。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>但一般简单的语法可以直接嵌入语义动作处理就</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>ok</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>了，比如这个</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>demo</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>语义动作一般是以包含在</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>{}</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>的目标语言的代码。具体的规范参照</span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>: (http://www.antlr.org/wiki/display/ANTLR3/Grammars)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'>本节就针对重点地地方进行代码注释。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:
宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:
AR-SA'>prog</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>:<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span>stat+ ;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>stat:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span class=SpellE>expr</span>
NEWLINE {<span class=SpellE>System.out.println</span>($<span class=SpellE>expr.value</span>);}
//</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>打印匿名表达式值，<span
lang=EN-US>$<span class=SpellE>expr</span></span>是引用这个<span class=SpellE><span
lang=EN-US>expr</span></span>这个语法元素，</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:red;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>需要注意的是<span lang=EN-US> value</span>并不是<span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>expr</span></span>的内建的属性，而是自定义的<span lang=EN-US>return</span>的值</span><span
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>，参见<span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>expr</span></span>的语法表达式。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>|<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>ID '=' <span class=SpellE>expr</span>
NEWLINE<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>{<span
class=SpellE>memory.put</span>($<span class=SpellE>ID.text</span>, new
Integer($<span class=SpellE>expr.value</span>));} //</span><span
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>命名表达式的值存入一个<span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>hashmap</span></span>对象。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>|<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>NEWLINE<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:
宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:
AR-SA'>expr</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'> returns [<span class=SpellE>int</span> value] //</span><span
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>在此定义了这个<span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>expr</span></span>对调用者提供一个<span lang=EN-US>value</span>的返回值。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>e=<span class=SpellE>multExpr</span>
{$value = $<span class=SpellE>e.value</span>;} //</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>以<span lang=EN-US>e</span>的方式引用第一个<span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>multExpr</span></span><span lang=EN-US>,</span>语义动作在此把左边的表达式的值赋给返回值变量。注意<span
lang=EN-US>:$<span class=SpellE>e.value</span></span>也不是内建的，是<span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>multExpr</span></span>定义的返回值。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span>(<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'+' e=<span
class=SpellE>multExpr</span> {$value += $<span class=SpellE>e.value</span>;}//</span><span
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>以<span
lang=EN-US>e</span>的方式第二个<span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>multExpr</span></span>，由于作用域不同，故无冲突，这个语义动作只有遇到<span
lang=EN-US>+</span>才会执行。语义动作式返回值累加<span lang=EN-US>e</span>这个项。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span>|<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>'-' e=<span
class=SpellE>multExpr</span> {$value -= $<span class=SpellE>e.value</span>;}//</span><span
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;
color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>同理，不过是累减。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>)*<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>//</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>需要特别注意的是，这个克林闭包，会让上面的两个语义动作，不断的重复。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:
宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:
AR-SA'>multExpr</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'> returns [<span class=SpellE>int</span> value]<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>//</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>这个表达式和<span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>expr</span></span><span
lang=EN-US> </span>无啥本质差别<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>e=atom {$value = $<span
class=SpellE>e.value</span>;} ('*' e=atom {$value *= $<span class=SpellE>e.value</span>;})*<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>; <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>atom returns
[<span class=SpellE>int</span> value]<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:
宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>:<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>INT {$value = <span class=SpellE>Integer.parseInt</span>($<span
class=SpellE>INT.text</span>);}//</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;
mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>将词法的字符串值转换成整型，然后赋值给返回值，<span lang=EN-US>text</span>是内建变量。<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
normal;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:

</span>Integer v = (Integer)<span class=SpellE>memory.get</span>($<span
class=SpellE>ID.text</span>);<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:

v!=null ) $value = <span class=SpellE>v.intValue</span>();<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:

<span class=SpellE>System.err.println</span>(&quot;undefined variable &quot;+$<span
class=SpellE>ID.text</span>);<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:

color:black;mso-fareast-language:ZH-CN;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'>如果是标识符，则从<span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>hashmap</span></span>中按名取出来。<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:
